          [
         </span>
         105
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1986">
       1986
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: 1986">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Suzy_Lamplugh" title="Disappearance of Suzy Lamplugh">
        Suzy Lamplugh
       </a>
       (25), British
       <a href="/wiki/Estate_agent" title="Estate agent">
        estate agent
       </a>
       , disappeared from
       <a href="/wiki/Fulham" title="Fulham">
        Fulham
       </a>
       , west
       <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">
        London
       </a>
       . In 1994, she was declared dead, presumed murdered. Despite further police investigations in 1998 and 2000, no trace of her has ever been found.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Philip_Cairns" title="Philip Cairns">
        Philip Cairns
       </a>
       (13), Irish schoolboy, disappeared in October 1986 on his way back to school after going home for lunch. His schoolbag was found abandoned in a previously searched lane near his house a few days later, but there has been no trace of Philip, and no arrests have ever been made in connection with the case.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Agust%C3%ADn_Feced" title="Agustn Feced">
        Agustn Feced
       </a>
       , 65, an Argentinian police official believed responsible for many tortures and extrajudicial executions during the country's
       <a href="/wiki/Dirty_War" title="Dirty War">
        Dirty War
       </a>
       , was stated to have died in prison on July 21 while facing charges related to those activities. However, the records of his death and burial are incomplete and sometimes contradictory. Several sources doubt he was even imprisoned at the time, and others claim to have seen him alive over the next ten years.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1987">
       1987
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: 1987">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Federico_Caff%C3%A8" title="Federico Caff">
        Federico Caff
       </a>
       (73), Italian economist, suddenly disappeared on the dawn of 15 April, shortly after quitting university teaching. He was declared dead on 30 October 1998. The mystery of his disappearance has not been solved.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1988">
       1988
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: 1988">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Ron_Arad_(pilot)" title="Ron Arad (pilot)">
        Ron Arad
       </a>
       (30), Israeli jet-fighter navigator, was under Israeli intelligence sight from 16 October 1986 (the day he was captured by Amal Shiite forces in southern Lebanon), and until the early hours of 4 May 1988 (coincidentally his 30th birthday), when he abruptly vanished from the house he was held in, at the village of Nebbi Shiit. Several speculations regarding his fate and whereabouts have been made since, involving both Iran and Syria, but no hard piece of evidence to support these claims has been found to date.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Lee_Boxell" title="Disappearance of Lee Boxell">
        Lee Boxell
       </a>
       (15), disappeared near his home in
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cheam,_Surrey" title="Cheam, Surrey">
        Cheam, Surrey
       </a>
       , on 10 September 1988. He was on his way to a football match at
       <a href="/wiki/Selhurst_Park" title="Selhurst Park">
        Selhurst Park
       </a>
       and has not been seen since.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Tara_Calico" title="Tara Calico">
        Tara Calico
       </a>
       (19), disappeared near her home in
       <a href="/wiki/Belen,_New_Mexico" title="Belen, New Mexico">
        Belen, New Mexico
       </a>
       , on 20 September 1988. A Polaroid photo of a boy and girl, bound and gagged, surfaced on 15 June 1989, but hasn't been confirmed to be Tara.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Michaela_Garecht" title="Michaela Garecht">
        Michaela Garecht
       </a>
       (9), Abducted by an unidentified white male at a grocery store in
       <a href="/wiki/Hayward,_California" title="Hayward, California">
        Hayward, California
       </a>
       , on 19 November 1988.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1989">
       1989
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: 1989">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Jacob_Wetterling" title="Jacob Wetterling">
        Jacob Wetterling
       </a>
       (11) was abducted by a masked gunman while cycling home in the dark with his brother Trevor (10) and friend Aaron (11) after going to rent a video from a convenience store a 10-minute ride away from his home in
       <a href="/wiki/St._Joseph,_Minnesota" title="St. Joseph, Minnesota">
        St. Joseph, Minnesota
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-106">
        <a href="#cite_note-106">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         106
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Melissa_Brannen" title="Disappearance of Melissa Brannen">
        Melissa Brannen
       </a>
       (5) disappeared from the Woodside Apartments in
       <a href="/wiki/Lorton,_Virginia" title="Lorton, Virginia">
        Lorton, Virginia
       </a>
       , while attending a party held at the complex for its residents.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1990s">
       1990s
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: 1990s">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1990">
       1990
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: 1990">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Sarah_MacDiarmid" title="Disappearance of Sarah MacDiarmid">
        Sarah MacDiarmid
       </a>
       (23) disappeared from
       <a href="/wiki/Kananook_railway_station" title="Kananook railway station">
        Kananook railway station
       </a>
       , Melbourne, Australia.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Trevaline_Evans" title="Disappearance of Trevaline Evans">
        Trevaline Evans
       </a>
       (52) vanished without trace after leaving a note on the front door of her antiques shop in
       <a href="/wiki/Llangollen" title="Llangollen">
        Llangollen
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Denbighshire" title="Denbighshire">
        Denbighshire
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Wales" title="Wales">
        Wales
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">
        United Kingdom
       </a>
       , saying she would be "back in two minutes".
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Ames_Glover" title="Disappearance of Ames Glover">
        Ames Glover
       </a>
       , a 5-month-old boy, disappeared from the back seat of his father's car in west
       <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">
        London
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">
        England
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">
        United Kingdom
       </a>
       , on 5 February. He has never been found and no charges have been brought.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1991">
       1991
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: 1991">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Ben_Needham" title="Disappearance of Ben Needham">
        Ben Needham
       </a>
       , a 21-month-old boy, disappeared from the island of Kos in Greece on 24 July. He has never been found. It was believed that Needham was abducted, and several suspects in
       <a href="/wiki/Kos" title="Kos">
        Kos
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Veria" title="Veria">
        Veria
       </a>
       were suggested as being responsible, but no one was ever charged with abduction.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Michael_Dunahee" title="Michael Dunahee">
        Michael Dunahee
       </a>
       (4) disappeared from a school playground in
       <a href="/wiki/Victoria,_British_Columbia" title="Victoria, British Columbia">
        Victoria, British Columbia
       </a>
       , Canada. His parents were nearby, but no witnesses to his presumed abduction have ever been identified, and there have been no subsequent confirmed sightings of him.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-107">
        <a href="#cite_note-107">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         107
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1992">
       1992
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: 1992">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/The_Springfield_Three" title="The Springfield Three">
        The Springfield Three
       </a>
       , Sherrill Levitt (47), her daughter Suzie Streeter (19), and Suzie's friend Stacy McCall (18), disappeared from Levitt's home in
       <a href="/wiki/Springfield,_Missouri" title="Springfield, Missouri">
        Springfield, Missouri
       </a>
       . Suzie and Stacy had graduated from Kickapoo High School the day before, and had arrived at Levitt's home at around 2:00 am after a graduation party. It is being investigated as an apparent triple disappearance.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-108">
        <a href="#cite_note-108">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         108
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1994">
       1994
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: 1994">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Michael_Anthony_Hughes" title="Michael Anthony Hughes">
        Michael Anthony Hughes
       </a>
       (6) was kidnapped from his school in
       <a href="/wiki/Choctaw,_Oklahoma" title="Choctaw, Oklahoma">
        Choctaw, Oklahoma
       </a>
       , by his stepfather Franklin Delano Floyd.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-doenetwork.org_109-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-doenetwork.org-109">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         109
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       Authorities have received conflicting reports from Floyd as to whether Hughes was murdered or is still alive and safe in the custody of an undisclosed caregiver. Hughes' mother died several years prior to his abduction. In addition to being his wife, she was raised by Floyd from an early age and was herself a kidnap victim.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-doenetwork.org_109-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-doenetwork.org-109">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         109
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Ylenia_Carrisi" title="Ylenia Carrisi">
        Ylenia Carrisi
       </a>
       (23), Italian
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/TV" title="TV">
        TV
       </a>
       celebrity, the daughter of singers
       <a href="/wiki/Albano_Carrisi" title="Albano Carrisi">
        Albano Carrisi
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Romina_Power" title="Romina Power">
        Romina Power
       </a>
       and the granddaughter of the American actor
       <a href="/wiki/Tyrone_Power" title="Tyrone Power">
        Tyrone Power
       </a>
       , disappeared during a vacation in
       <a href="/wiki/New_Orleans" title="New Orleans">
        New Orleans
       </a>
       .
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1995">
       1995
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: 1995">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Kiplyn_Davis" title="Kiplyn Davis">
        Kiplyn Davis
       </a>
       (15) was a high school student who was reported missing on 2 May 1995, in Spanish Fork, Utah. She is a featured child of the Polly Klaas Foundation. Several people have been arrested in connection with her murder, although no body has ever been found to confirm the girl's death.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-110">
        <a href="#cite_note-110">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         110
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Morgan_Nick" title="Disappearance of Morgan Nick">
        Morgan Nick
       </a>
       (6) was at a Little League baseball game with her mother in
       <a href="/wiki/Alma,_Arkansas" title="Alma, Arkansas">
        Alma, Arkansas
       </a>
       , when she was believed to have been abducted by a man she was seen with earlier. Her mother started the Morgan Nick Foundation for missing children.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Jodi_Huisentruit" title="Jodi Huisentruit">
        Jodi Huisentruit
       </a>
       (27),
       <a href="/wiki/KIMT" title="KIMT">
        KIMT
       </a>
       news anchor, was abducted from outside her apartment while on her way to work in
       <a href="/wiki/Mason_City,_Iowa" title="Mason City, Iowa">
        Mason City, Iowa
       </a>
       . She was declared legally dead in 2001.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-111">
        <a href="#cite_note-111">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         111
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Richey_Edwards" title="Richey Edwards">
        Richey Edwards
       </a>
       (27), a member of Welsh
       <a href="/wiki/Rock_music" title="Rock music">
        rock
       </a>
       band
       <a href="/wiki/Manic_Street_Preachers" title="Manic Street Preachers">
        Manic Street Preachers
       </a>
       , had a history of
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Self-injury" title="Self-injury">
        self-injury
       </a>
       and received treatment for
       <a href="/wiki/Alcoholism" title="Alcoholism">
        alcoholism
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Anorexia_nervosa" title="Anorexia nervosa">
        anorexia nervosa
       </a>
       , and
       <a href="/wiki/Major_depressive_disorder" title="Major depressive disorder">
        depression
       </a>
       in the years leading up to his disappearance. His car was found abandoned at the
       <a href="/wiki/Severn_View_services" title="Severn View services">
        Aust service area
       </a>
       adjacent to the
       <a href="/wiki/Severn_Bridge" title="Severn Bridge">
        Severn Bridge
       </a>
       , a location notorious for suicides.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-112">
        <a href="#cite_note-112">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         112
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       He was
       <a href="/wiki/Declared_death_in_absentia" title="Declared death in absentia">
        declared dead
       </a>
       in November 2008.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-113">
        <a href="#cite_note-113">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         113
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Gedhun_Choekyi_Nyima" title="Gedhun Choekyi Nyima">
        Gedhun Choekyi Nyima
       </a>
       (6), a boy recognized by the
       <a href="/wiki/Dalai_Lama" title="Dalai Lama">
        Dalai Lama
       </a>
       as being the 11th
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Panchen_lama" title="Panchen lama">
        Panchen lama
       </a>
       (a reincarnation of the 10th panchen lama).
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-114">
        <a href="#cite_note-114">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         114
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-buddhistchannel.tv_115-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-buddhistchannel.tv-115">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         115
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       His whereabouts are unknown.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116">
        <a href="#cite_note-116">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         116
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-117">
        <a href="#cite_note-117">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         117
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Dor_Bahadur_Bista" title="Dor Bahadur Bista">
        Dor Bahadur Bista
       </a>
       , a prominent anthropologist from
       <a href="/wiki/Nepal" title="Nepal">
        Nepal
       </a>
       , disappeared from
       <a href="/wiki/Jumla_District" title="Jumla District">
        Jumla District
       </a>
       in January 1995.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-118">
        <a href="#cite_note-118">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         118
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1996">
       1996
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: 1996">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Claremont_serial_murders" title="Claremont serial murders">
        Sarah Spiers
       </a>
       (18) disappeared after leaving a nightclub in
       <a href="/wiki/Claremont,_Western_Australia" title="Claremont, Western Australia">
        Claremont, Western Australia
       </a>
       , in January 1996. Her body has never been found. Almost six months later, Jane Rimmer, 23, disappeared from the same part of Claremont. Her remains were found in a southern Perth suburb in August 1996. A third victim, Ciara Glennon (27), also disappeared from Claremont in March 1997, with her remains being found three weeks later in a northern Perth suburb. The cases became known as the
       <a href="/wiki/Claremont_serial_murders" title="Claremont serial murders">
        Claremont serial murders
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Kristin_Smart" title="Disappearance of Kristin Smart">
        Kristin Smart
       </a>
       (19), a student at
       <a href="/wiki/California_Polytechnic_State_University" title="California Polytechnic State University">
        California Polytechnic State University
       </a>
       , disappeared after leaving a party. As a result of her disappearance, Cal Poly received criticism for not treating Smart's disappearance as a potential crime, and possibly pertinent evidence was destroyed when the university allowed students' rooms to be cleaned before police investigated.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Susan_Walsh" title="Disappearance of Susan Walsh">
        Susan Walsh
       </a>
       (36), freelance journalist, was last seen leaving her
       <a href="/wiki/Nutley,_New_Jersey" title="Nutley, New Jersey">
        Nutley, New Jersey
       </a>
       , apartment on 16 July to run some errands. Her disappearance was widely publicized; it is believed to possibly be linked to the Russian mafia due to her work investigating human trafficking in the sex trades.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1997">
       1997
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: 1997">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Angelo_Cruz" title="Angelo Cruz">
        Angelo Cruz
       </a>
       (39), a New York-born Puerto Rican basketball player who returned to home land Puerto Rico to visit family. No sightings of him have been recorded since.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Grant_Hadwin" title="Grant Hadwin">
        Grant Hadwin
       </a>
       (48), an anti-logging activist, went missing February 13 while traveling by kayak across the
       <a href="/wiki/Hecate_Strait" title="Hecate Strait">
        Hecate Strait
       </a>
       to
       <a href="/wiki/Graham_Island" title="Graham Island">
        Graham Island
       </a>
       in Canada. The wreckage of the kayak was discovered in June, but no trace of Hadwin himself has been found.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-119">
        <a href="#cite_note-119">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         119
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Robert_Durst#Other_cases" title="Robert Durst">
        Kristen Modaferri
       </a>
       (18), was last seen leaving the
       <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco" title="San Francisco">
        San Francisco
       </a>
       coffee shop where she worked on 23 June.
       <a href="/wiki/Robert_Durst" title="Robert Durst">
        Robert Durst
       </a>
       , suspected of several other disappearances of women, including his first wife, has been suspected in this one as well since he is believed to have been living in San Francisco at the time and is known to have disguised himself by posing as a woman, as police believe an unidentified suspect in this case did. Modaferri's disappearance led her parents to establish the
       <a href="/wiki/National_Center_for_Missing_Adults" title="National Center for Missing Adults">
        National Center for Missing Adults
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LAist_120-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-LAist-120">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         120
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       Manhattan artists Camden Sylvia (36) and Michael Sullivan (54) left their
       <a href="/wiki/Pearl_Street_(Manhattan)" title="Pearl Street (Manhattan)">
        Pearl Street
       </a>
       apartment to go running on November 7, 1997, and have not been seen since. They had been having a dispute with their landlord, Robert Rodriguez, over the heat at the time. Rodriguez initially cooperated with police but then stopped; extensive searches of his property in the city and
       <a href="/wiki/Upstate_New_York" title="Upstate New York">
        upstate
       </a>
       turned up nothing. He later served a short prison sentence on other charges.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Pearl_Street_mystery_121-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Pearl_Street_mystery-121">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         121
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Robert_Durst#Other_cases" title="Robert Durst">
        Karen Mitchell
       </a>
       (16) was last seen talking to someone in a car in her hometown of
       <a href="/wiki/Eureka,_California" title="Eureka, California">
        Eureka, California
       </a>
       on 25 November 1997. Robert Durst, also a person of interest in this case, was known to be in that area on that day and had previously visited the homeless shelter where Mitchell worked while disguised as a woman. A sketch of the man Mitchell was last seen talking to also strongly resembles a bespectacled Durst.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CNNColdCases_122-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-CNNColdCases-122">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         122
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1998">
       1998
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: 1998">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Amy_Lynn_Bradley" title="Disappearance of Amy Lynn Bradley">
        Amy Lynn Bradley
       </a>
       (23), an American passenger on the
       <a href="/wiki/Royal_Caribbean_International" title="Royal Caribbean International">
        Royal Caribbean International
       </a>
       cruise ship
       <a href="/wiki/MS_Rhapsody_of_the_Seas" title="MS Rhapsody of the Seas">
        <i>
         Rhapsody of the Seas
        </i>
       </a>
       , disappeared while the ship was docking in
       <a href="/wiki/Cura%C3%A7ao" title="Curaao">
        Curaao
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Antilles" title="Antilles">
        Antilles
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-visitaruba_123-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-visitaruba-123">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         123
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Rui_Pedro_Teixeira_Mendon%C3%A7a" title="Rui Pedro Teixeira Mendona">
        Rui Pedro Teixeira Mendona
       </a>
       (11) is a Portuguese child who went missing on 4 March 1998 in Lousada, Portugal. Rui Pedro was 11 years old and riding his bicycle outside near his home when he disappeared. Despite numerous sightings and wide media coverage, his disappearance remains unsolved.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1999">
       1999
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: 1999">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Viktar_Hanchar" title="Viktar Hanchar">
        Viktar Hanchar
       </a>
       , 42, a
       <a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">
        Belarusian
       </a>
       opposition leader, disappeared along with his friend, businessman Anatoly Krasouski, from a street in
       <a href="/wiki/Minsk" title="Minsk">
        Minsk
       </a>
       on September 16. There were signs of a struggle where they were last seen; it is widely believed the two were abducted and later murdered.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2000s">
       2000s
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: 2000s">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2000">
       2000
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: 2000">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Zebb_Quinn" title="Disappearance of Zebb Quinn">
        Zebb Quinn
       </a>
       (20), disappeared 2 January 2000 in
       <a href="/wiki/Asheville,_North_Carolina" title="Asheville, North Carolina">
        Asheville, North Carolina
       </a>
       , after receiving a page from his aunt's phone number. She denies paging him, but told police that her home was broken into during that time frame. Nothing was stolen from her home, but items were moved around. His car resurfaced two weeks after his disappearance when it was mysteriously parked in front of his mother's workplace with a live puppy inside and a large set of lips drawn on the window. In 2015 Asheville detectives unearthed fabric, leather materials and "unknown hard fragments" that were buried under a layer of concrete on the property of Robert Jason Owens. Owens was the last person know to have seen Zebb and had given several conflicting stories to detectives in his case. The search of his property that uncovered this new evidence was conducted after he was arrested for an unrelated triple murder.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-124">
        <a href="#cite_note-124">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         124
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Leah_Roberts" title="Disappearance of Leah Roberts">
        Leah Roberts
       </a>
       (23), abruptly left her home in
       <a href="/wiki/Durham,_North_Carolina" title="Durham, North Carolina">
        Durham, North Carolina
       </a>
       on 9 March 2000. Her sister later found a note suggesting she was going on a cross-country road trip to northern
       <a href="/wiki/Washington_(state)" title="Washington (state)">
        Washington
       </a>
       ; a review of her banking and credit records confirmed this. Her car was found wrecked and abandoned nine days later off the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mount_Baker_Highway" title="Mount Baker Highway">
        Mount Baker Highway
       </a>
       in
       <a href="/wiki/Whatcom_County,_Washington" title="Whatcom County, Washington">
        Whatcom County
       </a>
       ; evidence found in it suggested she had arrived there several days earlier. Other than one report that she was seen walking disoriented around a gas station in
       <a href="/wiki/Everett,_Washington" title="Everett, Washington">
        Everett
       </a>
       shortly after her car was discovered, she has not been seen or heard from since.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Leah_Roberts_125-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Leah_Roberts-125">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         125
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Bruno_Manser" title="Bruno Manser">
        Bruno Manser
       </a>
       (45), a Swiss-born activist who fervently campaigned for the preservation of rainforests in
       <a href="/wiki/Sarawak" title="Sarawak">
        Sarawak
       </a>
       , was last seen in May 2000, in the isolated village of
       <a href="/wiki/Bario" title="Bario">
        Bario
       </a>
       in Sarawak, near the border with Indonesia. He was
       <a href="/wiki/Declared_death_in_absentia" title="Declared death in absentia">
        declared legally dead
       </a>
       in March 2005.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Rilya_Wilson" title="Rilya Wilson">
        Rilya Wilson
       </a>
       (4) was a foster child of the Florida Department of Children and Families (DCF) who was last seen in 2000. Because she was not discovered missing until 2002, she became the centerpoint of an investigation into neglect and mismanagement in the organization.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2001">
       2001
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: 2001">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jason_Jolkowski" title="Jason Jolkowski">
        Jason Jolkowski
       </a>
       (19), a resident of
       <a href="/wiki/Omaha,_Nebraska" title="Omaha, Nebraska">
        Omaha, Nebraska
       </a>
       , disappeared on 13 June, after failing to show up at a local high school where he'd arranged to catch a ride to work with a friend. A neighbor reported seeing Jolkowski carrying trash cans into his garage. This, the last confirmed sighting of Jolkowski, took place approximately 30 minutes prior to the arranged meeting at the high school.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-126">
        <a href="#cite_note-126">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         126
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       His parents subsequently founded Project Jason, a nonprofit organization that assists families of missing persons.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Sneha_Anne_Philip" title="Sneha Anne Philip">
        Sneha Anne Philip
       </a>
       (31) was an Indian-American physician last seen on 10 September 2001, on surveillance camera footage from a store near her Lower Manhattan apartment. Due to the proximity of the World Trade Center and her medical training, her family believes she perished trying to help victims of the next day's terrorist attack. A court has agreed and she is officially considered to have died that way. The ruling was not unanimous, and no proof of her death has ever been found.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYT_on_appeal_127-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-NYT_on_appeal-127">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         127
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2002">
       2002
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: 2002">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Bison_Dele" title="Bison Dele">
        Bison Dele
       </a>
       (33, born Brian Carson Williams), a former
       <a href="/wiki/National_Basketball_Association" title="National Basketball Association">
        NBA
       </a>
       player; his girlfriend Serena Karlan (30); and French skipper Bertrand Saldo (32) were last heard from on 6 July when they left the
       <a href="/wiki/French_Polynesia" title="French Polynesia">
        French Polynesian
       </a>
       island of
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Moorea" title="Moorea">
        Moorea
       </a>
       aboard Dele's 55ft (17m)
       <a href="/wiki/Catamaran" title="Catamaran">
        catamaran
       </a>
       ,
       <i>
        Hakuna Matata
       </i>
       , bound for
       <a href="/wiki/Honolulu" title="Honolulu">
        Honolulu
       </a>
       via the
       <a href="/wiki/Marquesas_Islands" title="Marquesas Islands">
        Marquesas Islands
       </a>
       .
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2003">
       2003
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: 2003">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ben_Charles_Padilla" title="Ben Charles Padilla">
        Ben Charles Padilla
       </a>
       (50), a licensed aircraft mechanic, flight engineer, and pilot of small airplanes, was on board
       <a href="/wiki/Boeing_727" title="Boeing 727">
        Boeing 727
       </a>
       -223 designation
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/N844AA" title="N844AA">
        N844AA
       </a>
       when it was stolen from
       <a href="/wiki/Quatro_de_Fevereiro_Airport" title="Quatro de Fevereiro Airport">
        Luanda
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Angola" title="Angola">
        Angola
       </a>
       , on 25 May and has not been heard from since.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-128">
        <a href="#cite_note-128">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         128
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Reda_Helal" title="Reda Helal">
        Reda Helal
       </a>
       , an Egyptian journalist. In 11 August 2003, he disappeared en route from
       <a href="/wiki/Al-Ahram" title="Al-Ahram">
        Al-Ahram
       </a>
       Newspaper's offices to his home in downtown
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cairo,_Egypt" title="Cairo, Egypt">
        Cairo
       </a>
       . He was presumably kidnapped.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Terrance_Williams_and_Felipe_Santos#Disappearance_of_Felipe_Santos" title="Disappearance of Terrance Williams and Felipe Santos">
        Felipe Santos
       </a>
       (24) Last seen being arrested for driving without a license after a traffic accident early on 1 October outside
       <a href="/wiki/Naples,_Florida" title="Naples, Florida">
        Naples, Florida
       </a>
       , by Collier County sheriff's deputy Steve Calkins. Jail records show he was never booked. Calkins claimed to have changed his mind and left Santos at a nearby Circle K convenience store. Three months later, another man, Terrance Williams, disappeared after being arrested by the same police officer.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-News-Press_two_disappearances_story_129-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-News-Press_two_disappearances_story-129">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         129
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2004">
       2004
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: 2004">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Heber_Jentzsch" title="Heber Jentzsch">
        Heber Jentzsch
       </a>
       , 69, president of the
       <a href="/wiki/Church_of_Scientology_International" title="Church of Scientology International">
        Church of Scientology International
       </a>
       has not been seen in public since this year.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Terrance_Williams_and_Felipe_Santos" title="Disappearance of Terrance Williams and Felipe Santos">
        Terrance Williams
       </a>
       (27) Last seen being arrested on 12 January in
       <a href="/wiki/Naples,_Florida" title="Naples, Florida">
        Naples, Florida
       </a>
       , by
       <a href="/wiki/Collier_County,_Florida" title="Collier County, Florida">
        Collier County
       </a>
       sheriff's deputy Steve Calkins. Terrance had also been driving without a license. Williams was never booked and Calkins claims to have changed his mind and left him at a nearby Circle K convenience store. Felipe Santos disappeared three months earlier under similar circumstances after being arrested by the same officer
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-News-Press_two_disappearances_story_129-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-News-Press_two_disappearances_story-129">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         129
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Maura_Murray" title="Disappearance of Maura Murray">
        Maura Murray
       </a>
       (21) of
       <a href="/wiki/Hanson,_Massachusetts" title="Hanson, Massachusetts">
        Hanson, Massachusetts
       </a>
       , a nursing student at the
       <a href="/wiki/University_of_Massachusetts_Amherst" title="University of Massachusetts Amherst">
        University of Massachusetts Amherst
       </a>
       , was last seen 9 February at the scene of a minor one-vehicle accident in which her car was immobilised after having crashed into a roadside snowbank on
       <a href="/wiki/New_Hampshire_Route_112" title="New Hampshire Route 112">
        New Hampshire Route 112
       </a>
       . Earlier on the day of her disappearance, she had lied to professors about a death in her family, saying she would be absent from class for a week.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-130">
        <a href="#cite_note-130">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         130
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-131">
        <a href="#cite_note-131">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         131
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       A schoolbus driver who happened upon Murray's crash site stopped to ask if she needed help; Murray declined. Upon returning home shortly thereafter, the driver called police anyway, but by the time responders arrived 10 minutes later, Murray had vanished. Her keys, bank and credit cards have never been located, despite extensive searches of her abandoned car and the neighboring wooded areas.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-132">
        <a href="#cite_note-132">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         132
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Somchai_Neelapaijit" title="Somchai Neelapaijit">
        Somchai Neelapaijit
       </a>
       (52), a Thai Muslim lawyer and human rights activist representing
       <a href="/wiki/South_Thailand_insurgency" title="South Thailand insurgency">
        South Thailand insurgency
       </a>
       terrorism suspects, was last seen in
       <a href="/wiki/Bangkok" title="Bangkok">
        Bangkok
       </a>
       . It may be a case of
       <a href="/wiki/Forced_disappearance" title="Forced disappearance">
        forced disappearance
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-133">
        <a href="#cite_note-133">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         133
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-134">
        <a href="#cite_note-134">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         134
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Iraena_Asher" title="Disappearance of Iraena Asher">
        Iraena Asher
       </a>
       (25), a
       <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">
        New Zealand
       </a>
       model, allegedly suffering from
       <a href="/wiki/Bipolar_disorder" title="Bipolar disorder">
        bipolar disorder
       </a>
       , disappeared in controversial circumstances at
       <a href="/wiki/Piha" title="Piha">
        Piha
       </a>
       , west of
       <a href="/wiki/Auckland" title="Auckland">
        Auckland
       </a>
       , on 11 October 2004.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Brianna_Maitland" title="Disappearance of Brianna Maitland">
        Brianna Maitland
       </a>
       (17) vanished after leaving her job as a dishwasher at the Black Lantern Inn in Vermont. Her car was discovered the next day near an abandoned house, about a mile away.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WCAX1_135-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-WCAX1-135">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         135
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       Maitland's personal belongings were found inside the vehicle, including a recent paycheck and her wallet. Authorities believe foul play to be involved in Maitland's case, and many theories are under consideration, including one that Maitland may have been smuggled across the nearby Canadian border.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136">
        <a href="#cite_note-136">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         136
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2005">
       2005
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: 2005">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Natalee_Holloway" title="Disappearance of Natalee Holloway">
        Natalee Holloway
       </a>
       (18), an American student from Alabama, was last seen leaving a nightclub in
       <a href="/wiki/Aruba" title="Aruba">
        Aruba
       </a>
       with three men, including
       <a href="/wiki/Joran_van_der_Sloot" title="Joran van der Sloot">
        Joran van der Sloot
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-visitaruba_123-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-visitaruba-123">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         123
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       She was declared dead in 2012.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Ray_Gricar" title="Ray Gricar">
        Ray Gricar
       </a>
       (59) was district attorney of
       <a href="/wiki/Centre_County,_Pennsylvania" title="Centre County, Pennsylvania">
        Centre County, Pennsylvania
       </a>
       , in the United States. On 15 April, he called his girlfriend, in whose house he resided, from his car, giving his location east of
       <a href="/wiki/Centre_Hall,_Pennsylvania" title="Centre Hall, Pennsylvania">
        Centre Hall
       </a>
       . His car was found the next day but he was never heard from again. His family had him declared legally dead in 2011.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-DailyTimes20110330_137-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-DailyTimes20110330-137">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         137
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       In September 2013, a reputed former Hell's Angels member told authorities that Gricar was killed by the gang as retaliation. In April 2014, it was reported that the Pennsylvania State police would be assuming lead investigatory role in the case.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138">
        <a href="#cite_note-138">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         138
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_George_Smith" title="Disappearance of George Smith">
        George Allen Smith
       </a>
       (26) of
       <a href="/wiki/Greenwich,_Connecticut" title="Greenwich, Connecticut">
        Greenwich, Connecticut
       </a>
       , in the United States, went missing in the eastern Mediterranean from the
       <a href="/wiki/Royal_Caribbean_International" title="Royal Caribbean International">
        Royal Caribbean International
       </a>
       cruise ship
       <a href="/wiki/MS_Brilliance_of_the_Seas" title="MS Brilliance of the Seas">
        Brilliance of the Seas
       </a>
       ten days after his wedding.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Rahma_el-Dennaoui" title="Disappearance of Rahma el-Dennaoui">
        Rahma el-Dennaoui
       </a>
       (1) disappeared from her home in
       <a href="/wiki/Lurnea,_New_South_Wales" title="Lurnea, New South Wales">
        Lurnea, New South Wales
       </a>
       , near
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sydney,_Australia" title="Sydney, Australia">
        Sydney, Australia
       </a>
       , in the early hours of 10 November. Despite a police search and appeals to the general public, no trace of her was found.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Tara_Grinstead" title="Disappearance of Tara Grinstead">
        Tara Grinstead
       </a>
       (30), a high school history teacher from
       <a href="/wiki/Ocilla,_Georgia" title="Ocilla, Georgia">
        Ocilla, Georgia
       </a>
       , United States, went missing on 22 October. Investigators identified no suspects. 27-year-old Andrew Haley, in a bizarre twist, posted anonymous videos wherein he claimed to be a serial killer responsible for the murders of 16 women. One of the victims detailed by Haley in the videos matched the case of Grinstead, but police investigation ultimately revealed the videos to be part of an elaborate hoax by Haley.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139">
        <a href="#cite_note-139">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         139
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       A latex glove found outside Grinstead's home revealed DNA, but to date, no match has been found.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-140">
        <a href="#cite_note-140">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         140
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2006">
       2006
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: 2006">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jorge_Julio_L%C3%B3pez" title="Jorge Julio Lpez">
        Jorge Julio Lpez
       </a>
       (77), a retired Argentine bricklayer, was kidnapped during
       <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">
        Argentina
       </a>
       's
       <a href="/wiki/National_Reorganization_Process" title="National Reorganization Process">
        National Reorganization Process
       </a>
       in the 1970s. In September 2006, Lpez disappeared after testifying in a trial against
       <a href="/wiki/Dirty_War" title="Dirty War">
        Dirty War
       </a>
       criminal
       <a href="/wiki/Miguel_Etchecolatz" title="Miguel Etchecolatz">
        Miguel Etchecolatz
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Sivasubramaniam_Raveendranath" title="Sivasubramaniam Raveendranath">
        Sivasubramaniam Raveendranath
       </a>
       (55),
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sri_Lankan_Tamil" title="Sri Lankan Tamil">
        Sri Lankan Tamil
       </a>
       academic and
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vice_Chancellor" title="Vice Chancellor">
        Vice Chancellor
       </a>
       of the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eastern_University_of_Sri_Lanka" title="Eastern University of Sri Lanka">
        Eastern University of Sri Lanka
       </a>
       , disappeared while attending a conference in
       <a href="/wiki/Colombo" title="Colombo">
        Colombo
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Jennifer_Kesse" title="Disappearance of Jennifer Kesse">
        Jennifer Kesse
       </a>
       (24) went missing in January 2006, near a shopping mall in
       <a href="/wiki/Orlando,_Florida" title="Orlando, Florida">
        Orlando, Florida
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Jessie_Foster" title="Disappearance of Jessie Foster">
        Jessie Foster
       </a>
       (21), a
       <a href="/wiki/Canadians" title="Canadians">
        Canadian
       </a>
       woman, disappeared in the
       <a href="/wiki/Las_Vegas_Valley" title="Las Vegas Valley">
        Las Vegas Valley
       </a>
       in
       <a href="/wiki/Nevada" title="Nevada">
        Nevada
       </a>
       in the United States.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141">
        <a href="#cite_note-141">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         141
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Sherlyn_Cadapan_and_Karen_Empe%C3%B1o" title="Disappearance of Sherlyn Cadapan and Karen Empeo">
        Sherlyn Cadapan (27) and Karen Empeo (20)
       </a>
       , a
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Community_organizer" title="Community organizer">
        community organizer
       </a>
       and
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Graduate_student" title="Graduate student">
        graduate student
       </a>
       respectively, were abducted by armed gunmen in a remote area of the Philippines on 26 June 2006. They have not been seen since.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-142">
        <a href="#cite_note-142">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         142
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Joe_Pichler" title="Joe Pichler">
        Joe Pichler
       </a>
       (18) is a former American actor missing since 5 January 2006.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Anthony_Zizzo" title="Anthony Zizzo">
        Anthony Zizzo
       </a>
       (71), alleged
       <a href="/wiki/Underboss" title="Underboss">
        underboss
       </a>
       of the
       <a href="/wiki/Chicago_Outfit" title="Chicago Outfit">
        Chicago Outfit
       </a>
       , disappeared 31 August. Police suspect he has been murdered, although he may instead have fled the jurisdiction voluntarily.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2007">
       2007
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: 2007">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Jim_Gray_(computer_scientist)" title="Jim Gray (computer scientist)">
        Jim Gray
       </a>
       (63),
       <a href="/wiki/Database" title="Database">
        database
       </a>
       pioneer,
       <a href="/wiki/Microsoft_Research" title="Microsoft Research">
        Microsoft Research
       </a>
       scientist, and
       <a href="/wiki/Turing_Award" title="Turing Award">
        Turing Award
       </a>
       winner, left
       <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco_Bay" title="San Francisco Bay">
        San Francisco Bay
       </a>
       in his 12m (39ft) sailboat
       <i>
        Tenacious
       </i>
       to scatter his mother's ashes at the
       <a href="/wiki/Farallon_Islands" title="Farallon Islands">
        Farallon Islands
       </a>
       , a wildlife refuge 43km (27mi) away, and was reported missing when he failed to return later the same day. No
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mayday_(distress_signal)" title="Mayday (distress signal)">
        Mayday
       </a>
       call was heard, his
       <a href="/wiki/Distress_radiobeacon" title="Distress radiobeacon">
        distress radiobeacon
       </a>
       was not activated, and, despite one of the most ambitious
       <a href="/wiki/Search_and_rescue" title="Search and rescue">
        search and rescue
       </a>
       missions of all time, no trace of Gray or his yacht has ever been found.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-143">
        <a href="#cite_note-143">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         143
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       In 2012 he was declared legally dead.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JG_DecDeath_CACM072012_144-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-JG_DecDeath_CACM072012-144">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         144
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Lisa_Stebic" title="Lisa Stebic">
        Lisa Stebic
       </a>
       , 37, was last seen by her husband at their
       <a href="/wiki/Plainfield,_Illinois" title="Plainfield, Illinois">
        Plainfield, Illinois
       </a>
       , home on April 30, while she was awaiting a ride to the local track where she worked out; he was working in the back. The two were going through a divorce at the time; police believe foul play was involved and consider him a suspect.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lisa_Stebic_145-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Lisa_Stebic-145">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         145
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Kaz_II" title="Kaz II">
         Kaz II
        </a>
       </i>
       , a 9.8m (32ft) catamaran, was found adrift with its three-man crew, owner Derek Batten (56) and brothers Peter Tunstead (69) and James Tunstead (63), missing. The yacht's sails were up and its engine running, and the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Global_positioning_system" title="Global positioning system">
        global positioning system
       </a>
       showed the yacht had been drifting since around the time of their last known radio contact, about 11 hours after they departed
       <a href="/wiki/Shute_Harbour" title="Shute Harbour">
        Shute Harbour
       </a>
       for
       <a href="/wiki/Townsville" title="Townsville">
        Townsville
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Queensland" title="Queensland">
        Queensland
       </a>
       , five days earlier.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-146">
        <a href="#cite_note-146">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         146
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Michele_Miscavige" title="Michele Miscavige">
        Michele Miscavige
       </a>
       , 36, wife of
       <a href="/wiki/Church_of_Scientology" title="Church of Scientology">
        Church of Scientology
       </a>
       head
       <a href="/wiki/David_Miscavige" title="David Miscavige">
        David Miscavige
       </a>
       , has not been seen since August 2007. Her husband and other church officials claim she has elected to do her church work privately; two missing persons reports filed with Los Angeles police have been closed as unfounded; at least one detective is claimed to have actually met and spoken with her. Scientology critics claim that if she is alive, she is being held against her will.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-147">
        <a href="#cite_note-147">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         147
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Madeleine_McCann" title="Disappearance of Madeleine McCann">
        Madeleine McCann
       </a>
       (3) disappeared after being left asleep in the unlocked ground-floor bedroom of her family's rented holiday apartment in the
       <a href="/wiki/Algarve" title="Algarve">
        Algarve
       </a>
       (Portugal) while her parents dined with friends at a local restaurant. There have been no confirmed
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sightings_following_the_disappearance_of_Madeleine_McCann" title="Sightings following the disappearance of Madeleine McCann">
        sightings of her
       </a>
       since then.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148">
        <a href="#cite_note-148">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         148
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       Despite a myriad of theories about what happened to the toddler, no substantial evidence leading to any one individual has surfaced. Despite this, in 2014 Scotland Yard was reportedly looking at 38 people of interest, as well as researching the backgrounds of 530 known sex offenders, including 59 regarded as high interest.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149">
        <a href="#cite_note-149">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         149
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Aeryn_Gillern" title="Disappearance of Aeryn Gillern">
        Aeryn M. J. Gillern
       </a>
       (34), an American research assistant at the United Nations Industrial Development Organization (UNIDO) in Vienna, disappeared under mysterious circumstances after a night out on the town.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Andrew_McAuley" title="Andrew McAuley">
        Andrew McAuley
       </a>
       (born 7 August 1968; presumed dead 912 February 2007) was an Australian adventurer best known for mountaineering and sea kayaking in remote parts of the world. He is presumed to have died following his disappearance at sea while attempting to kayak 1600km across the Tasman Sea in February 2007.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_and_alleged_murder_of_Elodia_Ghinescu" title="Disappearance and alleged murder of Elodia Ghinescu">
        Elodia Marilena Ghinescu
       </a>
       (39), a Romanian lawyer from Brasov, disappeared under mysterious circumstances on the evening of 29 August 2007. The case triggered a media frenzy for many years, including a dedicated reality TV show which investigated the disappearance. In 2013 her husband was sentenced to 21 years in prison although her body was never found and the evidence was scarce.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2008">
       2008
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: 2008">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Amy_Fitzpatrick" title="Disappearance of Amy Fitzpatrick">
        Amy Fitzpatrick
       </a>
       (15), an Irish-born teenager, was last seen in Mijas Costa in Mlaga, Spain. She had been babysitting with a friend on New Year's Eve. Fitzpatrick left at about 10:10pm that night and never arrived home, only a short distance away. She has not been seen or heard from since. Investigators are working on her case.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2009">
       2009
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: 2009">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Jure_%C5%A0terk" title="Jure terk">
        Jure terk
       </a>
       (72) regularly communicated with radio amateurs while sailing around the world, but all communications ceased around 1 January 2009, as reported by an Australian ham radio operator.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Stuff.co.nz_1390877_150-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Stuff.co.nz_1390877-150">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         150
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       His sailboat
       <i>
        Lunatic
       </i>
       was spotted on 26 January by a merchant vessel, the
       <i>
        Aida
       </i>
       , and it appeared abandoned. It was found adrift and abandoned on 30 April 2009, by the crew of science vessel
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/RV_Roger_Revelle" title="RV Roger Revelle">
        RV
        <i>
         Roger Revelle
        </i>
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151">
        <a href="#cite_note-151">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         151
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Claudia_Lawrence" title="Disappearance of Claudia Lawrence">
        Claudia Lawrence
       </a>
       (35) was last seen on 18 March 2009, near
       <a href="/wiki/Heworth,_York" title="Heworth, York">
        Heworth
       </a>
       in
       <a href="/wiki/York" title="York">
        York
       </a>
       , England.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Susan_Powell" title="Disappearance of Susan Powell">
        Susan Powell
       </a>
       (28) disappeared from her home in Utah in the United States under suspicious circumstances in December 2009.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Jim_Robinson_(boxer)" title="Jim Robinson (boxer)">
        Jim Robinson
       </a>
       (84), a former professional boxer notable for his bout with
       <a href="/wiki/Muhammad_Ali" title="Muhammad Ali">
        Muhammad Ali
       </a>
       in 1961, disappeared from the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Overtown,_Miami,_Florida" title="Overtown, Miami, Florida">
        Overtown
       </a>
       district of Miami.
       <a href="/wiki/ESPN" title="ESPN">
        ESPN
       </a>
       and autograph collectors have failed to locate him.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Craig_Arnold" title="Craig Arnold">
        Craig Arnold
       </a>
       (41), American poet, disappeared after a hike on the Japanese island
       <a href="/wiki/Kuchinoerabu-jima" title="Kuchinoerabu-jima">
        Kuchinoerabu-jima
       </a>
       . He is presumed to have died in a fall from a high cliff, but the body has never been found.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152">
        <a href="#cite_note-152">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         152
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2010">
       2010
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: 2010">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Kyron_Horman" title="Disappearance of Kyron Horman">
        Kyron Horman
       </a>
       (7), an American schoolboy, disappeared from his school in northwestern
       <a href="/wiki/Portland,_Oregon" title="Portland, Oregon">
        Portland, Oregon
       </a>
       . Searches beginning 4 June 2010, uncovered no evidence of his fate.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Lyle_and_Marie_McCann" title="Disappearance of Lyle and Marie McCann">
        Lyle (78) and Marie (77) McCann
       </a>
       , Canadian couple whose
       <a href="/wiki/Motorhome" title="Motorhome">
        motorhome
       </a>
       was found burnt in the woods near
       <a href="/wiki/Edson,_Alberta" title="Edson, Alberta">
        Edson, Alberta
       </a>
       . One suspect was charged with
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/First-degree_murder" title="First-degree murder">
        first-degree murder
       </a>
       charges in the death of the couple, though their bodies have yet to be found.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153">
        <a href="#cite_note-153">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         153
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2011">
       2011
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: 2011">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Alessia_and_Livia_Schepp" title="Disappearance of Alessia and Livia Schepp">
        Alessia and Livia Schepp
       </a>
       (6) from St. Sulpice, a suburb of
       <a href="/wiki/Lausanne" title="Lausanne">
        Lausanne
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">
        Switzerland
       </a>
       , were twin sisters picked up for the weekend from their mother's home by their father, Mathias Kaspar Schepp, on 28 January 2011. The father was found dead a few days later, having apparently committed suicide.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Rebecca_Coriam" title="Disappearance of Rebecca Coriam">
        Rebecca Coriam
       </a>
       (24), a crewmember aboard the cruise ship
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Disney_Wonder" title="Disney Wonder">
         Disney Wonder
        </a>
       </i>
       , was last seen on 22 March 2011, when a security camera in the crew lounge recorded her having an upsetting telephone conversation. Some reports suggest she went overboard, but there is other evidence that she may have been alive in the following May.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Lauren_Spierer" title="Disappearance of Lauren Spierer">
        Lauren Spierer
       </a>
       (20), a student at Indiana University, disappeared in Bloomington, Indiana, on 3 June, after a night of partying at a local bar. The coed left a gathering at a housing complex alone in the early morning hours while highly intoxicated. Her disappearance generated national press coverage. In 2014, Spierer's parents filed a lawsuit against two individuals with whom Spierer had socialized on the evening before her disappearance. A federal judge dismissed the suit.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154">
        <a href="#cite_note-154">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         154
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Lisa_Irwin" title="Disappearance of Lisa Irwin">
        Lisa Irwin
       </a>
       (2) was reported missing from her home in Kansas City, Missouri, on 4 October 2011.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Lind_Lagerl%C3%B6f" title="Daniel Lind Lagerlf">
        Daniel Lind Lagerlf
       </a>
       (42), a Swedish director and screenwriter, disappeared at Tjurpannans Nature Reserve outside
       <a href="/wiki/Tanumshede" title="Tanumshede">
        Tanumshede
       </a>
       in
       <a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">
        Sweden
       </a>
       during preparations for the filming of
       <a href="/wiki/Camilla_L%C3%A4ckberg" title="Camilla Lckberg">
        Camilla Lckberg
       </a>
       's
       <i>
        Fjllbackamorden  Strandriddaren
       </i>
       . The search for him was suspended after two days without result.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155">
        <a href="#cite_note-155">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         155
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Erica_Parsons" title="Disappearance of Erica Parsons">
        Erica Parsons
       </a>
       (13), was last seen in North Carolina by persons outside her family in November 2011.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156">
        <a href="#cite_note-156">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         156
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Ayla_Reynolds" title="Disappearance of Ayla Reynolds">
        Ayla Reynolds
       </a>
       (1) was not in her bed on the morning of December 17. She had last been seen the night before in her father's
       <a href="/wiki/Waterville,_Maine" title="Waterville, Maine">
        Waterville, Maine
       </a>
       , home, by his sister or girlfriend, both of whom were also in residence. The search for the 20-month-old was the largest missing-persons investigation in the state's history. Police have evidence from the house suggesting foul play and believe her to be dead; however the body has not been found and no arrests have been made.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ayla_Reynolds_157-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Ayla_Reynolds-157">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         157
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2012">
       2012
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: 2012">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Guma_Aguiar" title="Guma Aguiar">
        Guma Aguiar
       </a>
       (35),
       <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">
        Brazilian
       </a>
       -born American industrialist and part-owner of Israel's
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Beitar_Jerusalem" title="Beitar Jerusalem">
        Beitar Jerusalem
       </a>
       football club, was last seen leaving his home in
       <a href="/wiki/Fort_Lauderdale,_Florida" title="Fort Lauderdale, Florida">
        Fort Lauderdale, Florida
       </a>
       , on 19 June. The next day his fishing boat, the
       <i>
        T.T. Zion
       </i>
       , was found with lights on and engines running, having gone aground on a local beach. His wallet and cell phone were on board. Two weeks of searches failed to find any trace of him.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Guma_Aguiar_158-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Guma_Aguiar-158">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         158
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Emma_Fillipoff" title="Emma Fillipoff">
        Emma Fillipoff
       </a>
       (26) disappeared on 28 November 2012 from in front of
       <a href="/wiki/The_Empress_(hotel)" title="The Empress (hotel)">
        The Empress Hotel
       </a>
       , in Victoria, B.C., Canada, after a 45-minute conversation with
       <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Police_Department" title="Victoria Police Department">
