        Victoria Police
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Sombath_Somphone" title="Sombath Somphone">
        Sombath Somphone
       </a>
       (60), Laotian community activist who disappeared on Saturday the 15th of December around 6 pm at a
       <a href="/wiki/Vientiane" title="Vientiane">
        Vientiane
       </a>
       police post after having been stopped while driving behind his wife's car.
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/CCTV" title="CCTV">
        CCTV
       </a>
       footage showed a motorcyclist getting off his bike and driving Somphone's car away, and a white truck approaching and subsequently driving off with Somphone.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-159">
        <a href="#cite_note-159">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         159
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Solved_cases">
       Solved cases
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_people_who_disappeared_mysteriously&amp;action=edit&amp;section=63" title="Edit section: Solved cases">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      This is a list of people who were previously listed above but have since been located.
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       The biologist
       <a href="/wiki/Margie_Profet" title="Margie Profet">
        Margie Profet
       </a>
       ceased contact with her family in 2002 and had last been seen in 2005. In May 2012 she was told by a friend about her "disappearance" and contacted her family. She had been living in an isolated location, suffering from a physical ailment that caused her severe pain, and had not realized she was considered "missing".
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-160">
        <a href="#cite_note-160">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         160
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-161">
        <a href="#cite_note-161">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         161
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Daniel_Morcombe" title="Daniel Morcombe">
        Daniel Morcombe
       </a>
       disappeared from the roadside near his
       <a href="/wiki/Sunshine_Coast,_Queensland" title="Sunshine Coast, Queensland">
        Sunshine Coast, Queensland
       </a>
       , Australia, home in 2003. His remains were found in 2011;
       <a href="/wiki/Brett_Peter_Cowan" title="Brett Peter Cowan">
        Brett Peter Cowan
       </a>
       was convicted of murder in the case.
      </li>
      <li>
       Russian media magnate
       <a href="/wiki/Leonid_Rozhetskin" title="Leonid Rozhetskin">
        Leonid Rozhetskin
       </a>
       disappeared from his home in
       <a href="/wiki/J%C5%ABrmala" title="Jrmala">
        Jrmala
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Latvia" title="Latvia">
        Latvia
       </a>
       , in 2008, widely assumed to be the victim of a political murder plot.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-162">
        <a href="#cite_note-162">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         162
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       His remains were found in a Latvian forest in 2012 and positively identified in November 2013.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-163">
        <a href="#cite_note-163">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         163
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       The four members of the
       <a href="/wiki/McStay_family_murder" title="McStay family murder">
        McStay family
       </a>
       abruptly disappeared from their
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fallbrook" title="Fallbrook">
        Fallbrook
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">
        California
       </a>
       home under suspicious circumstances on 4 February 2010.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-164">
        <a href="#cite_note-164">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         164
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nbcsandiego1_165-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nbcsandiego1-165">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         165
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       After much speculation on their whereabouts, their bodies were found by a biker in the desert near
       <a href="/wiki/Victorville,_California" title="Victorville, California">
        Victorville, California
       </a>
       on 13 November 2013. On 7 November 2014, police arrested Charles "Chase" Merritt, Joseph McStay's business partner, and charged him with the murders.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Los_Angeles_Times_166-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Los_Angeles_Times-166">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         166
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Murder_of_Holly_Bobo" title="Murder of Holly Bobo">
        Holly Bobo
       </a>
       disappeared from her home in
       <a href="/wiki/Parsons,_Tennessee" title="Parsons, Tennessee">
        Parsons, Tennessee
       </a>
       , in 2011. Her skull was found in September 2014.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Murder_of_Hannah_Graham" title="Murder of Hannah Graham">
        Hannah Graham
       </a>
       was last seen at the
       <a href="/wiki/Downtown_Mall" title="Downtown Mall">
        Downtown Mall
       </a>
       in Charlottesville, Virginia, on 13 September 2014. Her remains were found on 18 October 2014. Jesse Matthew was charged with her abduction.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Gavin_Smith_(film_studio_executive)" title="Gavin Smith (film studio executive)">
        Gavin Smith
       </a>
       (57), an executive with
       <a href="/wiki/20th_Century_Fox" title="20th Century Fox">
        20th Century Fox
       </a>
       , was last seen leaving a friend's house in
       <a href="/wiki/Oak_Park,_California" title="Oak Park, California">
        Oak Park, California
       </a>
       , on 1 May 2012.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Gavin_Smith_disappearance_167-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Gavin_Smith_disappearance-167">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         167
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       In 2014 he was declared legally dead from the night of his disappearance.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Gavin_Smith_legally_dead_story_168-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Gavin_Smith_legally_dead_story-168">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         168
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       His body was found later that year by hikers in a rural area near
       <a href="/wiki/Angeles_National_Forest" title="Angeles National Forest">
        Angeles National Forest
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-169">
        <a href="#cite_note-169">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         169
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       In early 2015 police arrested an imprisoned drug dealer whose wife Smith had been involved with and charged him with the murder.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LA_Times_Creech_story_170-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-LA_Times_Creech_story-170">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         170
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Lucy_Ann_Johnson" title="Lucy Ann Johnson">
        Lucy Ann Johnson
       </a>
       disappeared in 1961 but was not reported missing until 1965. She was found alive with a new family in 2013.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-171">
        <a href="#cite_note-171">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         171
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Disappearance_of_Charles_Bothuell_V" title="Disappearance of Charles Bothuell V">
        Charles Bothuell V
       </a>
       , is an American teenager from
       <a href="/wiki/Detroit" title="Detroit">
        Detroit
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Michigan" title="Michigan">
        Michigan
       </a>
       that was reported missing, but found days later by members of law enforcement, to the surprise of his father, Charles Bothuell IV, in his basement.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-172">
        <a href="#cite_note-172">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         172
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>

        <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
         <b>
          <a href="#cite_ref-16">
           ^
          </a>
         </b>
        </span>
        <span class="reference-text">
